4. 3  B e n d a  m usti n e i n   D  L  B  C  L   T r e at  m e nt  
B e n d a  m usti n e (  B E  N ) is  a  c h e  m ot h er a p e uti c  a g e nt, s y nt h esis e d  as  a  h y bri d  of  a  p uri n e  a n al o g u e a n d  a n  al k yl at or. bet wee n t he enr ol me nt s of tw o c o nsec uti ve p atie nts (c o u nte d fr o m C 1 D 4).

(a p pr o xi matel y 6 patie nts in t otal) the safet y data w ill be re vie we d b y t he I D M C.
